Switzerland is famed for its breathtaking Alpine scenery, azure lakes, quaint medieval towns and thriving economy. Below are the top 4 destinations in Switzerland:\n\nThe city of Lucerne \nThe city of Lucerne is situated on the shores of the picturesque Lake Lucerne, home to the world-famous Chapel Bridge. The old town\u2019s architecture dating back to the 17th century, clock tower, lion statue, makes Lucerne an idyllic tourist city. Visitors can stroll along the lake, take in the magnificent mountain views or savor traditional Swiss cuisine.\n\nGeneva\nGeneva, the capital of the canton of Geneva, is the largest city in Switzerland. The city boasts unique Renaissance and Baroque architecture alongside countless upscale restaurants and hotels.\n\nThe charming village of Zermatt\nThe charming village of Zermatt lies at the foot of the iconic Matterhorn peak. It is a paradise for skiing and mountaineering. Visitors can admire Zermatt\u2019s breathtaking views from atop Gornergrat at 3,089m when taking the cable car ride. The traditional wood houses with red rooftops make a memorable impression.\n\nInterlaken\nInterlaken is a popular resort town nestled between two jewel-toned lakes, Thun and Brienz.
